view : panel id : DVRIP: Company: Panel Make: ATMID: From Date: To Date:
SELECT a.Customer,a.Bank,a.ATMID,a.ATMShortName,a.SiteAddress,a.DVRIP,a.Panel_make,a.zone as zon,a.City,a.State,b.id,b.panelid,b.createtime,b.receivedtime,b.comment,b.zone,b.alarm,b.closedBy,b.closedtime,b.sendip FROM sites a,`alerts` b WHERE (a.OldPanelID=b.panelid or a.NewPanelID=b.panelid) and a.DVRIP='10.109.9.171' and b.receivedtime between '2022-09-30 00:00:00' and '2022-09-30 23:59:59' order by receivedtime desc;
